        network 100 create
            description "NETWORK QoS POLICY Ingress classification,Egress remarking "
            ingress
                default-action fc be profile in
                dscp be fc be profile out
                dscp cs1 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs2 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs3 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs4 fc h2 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc ef profile in
                dscp nc1 fc h2 profile in
                dscp nc2 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile out
                lsp-exp 1 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 5 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc ef profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc ef
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                exit
                fc h2
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                exit
            exit
        exit
        network 200 create
            description "Network QoS policy ingress need mark"
            ingress
                default-action fc ef profile in
                dscp be fc be profile in
                dscp cs1 fc l1 profile in
                dscp cs2 fc l1 profile in
                dscp cs3 fc l1 profile in
                dscp cs4 fc h1 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc ef profile in
                dscp nc1 fc nc profile in
                dscp nc2 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile in
                lsp-exp 1 fc l1 profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc l1 profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc l1 profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc h1 profile in
                lsp-exp 5 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc nc profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc ef profile in
                dot1p 0 fc ef profile in
                dot1p 1 fc l1 profile in
                dot1p 2 fc l1 profile in
                dot1p 3 fc l1 profile in
                dot1p 4 fc h1 profile in
                dot1p 5 fc ef profile in
                dot1p 6 fc nc profile in
                dot1p 7 fc ef profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc ef
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                exit
                fc h1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 4
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                    dot1p-in-profile 4
                    dot1p-out-profile 4
                exit
                fc l1
                    dscp-in-profile cs1
                    dscp-out-profile cs1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 1
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 1
                    dot1p-in-profile 1
                    dot1p-out-profile 1
                exit
                fc nc
                    dscp-in-profile nc1
                    dscp-out-profile nc1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                    dot1p-in-profile 6
                    dot1p-out-profile 6
                exit
